      <h2>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Lunar_eclipses_between_-1599_and_-1500">
        Lunar eclipses between -1599 and -1500
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_16th-century_BCE_lunar_eclipses&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Lunar eclipses between -1599 and -1500">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h2>
      <p>
       There were 226
       <a href="/wiki/Lunar_eclipse" title="Lunar eclipse">
        lunar eclipse
       </a>
       events between -1599 and -1500 (1600 BCE to 1501 BCE)
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-1">
        <a href="#cite_note-1">
         [1]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
